Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 210 (Apollo 15-17 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Jim Lawton, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 210 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY 
	BY NASA 2021112-161 17:11 MAR. 19,1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

022373,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              rewritten, and there are other small changes here and there.

022384,000030:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
022385,000031:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022386,000032:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022387,000033:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022388,000034:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022389,000035: 
022390,000036:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
022391,000037:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
022392,000038:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
022393,000039:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
022394,000040:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022395,000041: 
022396,000042:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
022397,000043:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022398,000044:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
022399,000045:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
022400,000046:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
022401,000047:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
022402,000048:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
022403,000049:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
022404,000050:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
022405,000051:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
022406,000052:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)    
022407,000053:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
022408,000054:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022409,000055:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022410,000056:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022411,000057:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022412,000058:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
022413,000059:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022414,000060:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
022415,000061:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022416,000062:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022417,000063:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
022418,000064:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022419,000065:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
022420,000066: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
022421,000067: 
022422,000068: 33,2113                                           BANK     33                                    
022423,000069: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
022424,000070: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
022425,000071: 
022426,000072: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022427,000073: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
022428,000074: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
022429,000075: 24,2000           05331        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022430,000076: 24,2001           00004                           OCT      4                                     
022431,000077: 24,2002           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022432,000078: 24,2003           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022433,000079: 24,2004           02751                           TC       LUNSFCHK                              #  CHECK IF ON LUNAR SURFACE

022908,000554:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022909,000555:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022910,000556:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022911,000557:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022912,000558:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022913,000559: 
022914,000560:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022915,000561:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022916,000562:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022917,000563:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022918,000564:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022919,000565:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022920,000566:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022921,000567:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022922,000568:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022923,000569:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022924,000570:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022925,000571:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022926,000572:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022927,000573:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022928,000574:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022929,000575:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022930,000576:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022931,000577:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022932,000578:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022933,000579:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022934,000580:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022935,000581:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022936,000582: 24,2462  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022937,000583: 24,2462                                           COUNT*   $$/P25                                
022938,000584: 24,2462           05331        PROG25             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022939,000585: 24,2463           00004                           OCT      4                                     #  MAKE GROUP 4 INACTIVE (VERB 37)
022940,000586: 24,2464           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022941,000587: 24,2465           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022942,000588: 
022943,000589: 24,2466           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022944,000590: 24,2467           33757                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
022945,000591: 24,2470           05506                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022946,000592: 24,2471           00031                           ADRES    TRACKFLG                              #  SET TRACK FLAG
022947,000593: 24,2472           05506                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022948,000594: 24,2473           00006                           ADRES    P25FLAG                               #  SET P25FLAG
022949,000595: 24,2474           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              
022950,000596: 24,2475           00010                           ADRES    RNDVZFLG

022952,000598: 24,2477           04022                           OCT      04022

022954,000600: 24,2501           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 #  IS P25FLAG SET
022955,000601: 24,2502           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022956,000602: 24,2503           15146                           BZF      ENDOFJOB                              
022957,000603: 24,2504           34740                           CAF      TRACKBIT                              #  IS TRACKFLAG SET?

Page 519 

022959,000605: 24,2505           70075                           MASK     STATE      +1                         
022960,000606: 24,2506           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022961,000607: 24,2507           12515                           BZF      P25LMWT1                              #  NO-SKIP PHASE CHANGE AND WAIT 1 MINUTE
022962,000608: 24,2510           34750                           CAF      SEVEN                                 #  CALL R65 - FINE PREFERRED
022963,000609: 24,2511           55745                           TS       R65CNTR                               
022964,000610: 24,2512           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              #  TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE

022980,000626:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022981,000627:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022982,000628:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022983,000629:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022984,000630:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022985,000631: 
022986,000632:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022987,000633:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022988,000634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022989,000635:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022990,000636:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
022991,000637:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022992,000638:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
022993,000639:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
022994,000640:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
022995,000641:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022996,000642:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
022997,000643:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
022998,000644:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
022999,000645:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023000,000646:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
023001,000647:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
023002,000648:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023003,000649:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
023004,000650:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023005,000651:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
023006,000652:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023007,000653:                                                                                                  #    NOANGFLG
023008,000654:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

023183,000829:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
023184,000830:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023185,000831:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023186,000832:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023187,000833:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023188,000834: 
023189,000835:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
023190,000836:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
023191,000837:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023192,000838:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023193,000839:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
023194,000840:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
023195,000841:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
023196,000842:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
023197,000843:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
023198,000844:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
023199,000845:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
023200,000846:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
023201,000847:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
023202,000848:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023203,000849:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
023204,000850:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
023205,000851:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
023206,000852:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023207,000853:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023208,000854:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023209,000855:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
023210,000856:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET

023212,000858:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
023213,000859:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM

023388,001034:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
023389,001035:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023390,001036:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023391,001037:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023392,001038:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023393,001039: 
023394,001040:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023395,001041:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023396,001042:                                                                                                  #           TC     R23LEM
023397,001043:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023398,001044:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL        R61LEM
023399,001045:                                                                                                  #    SETMINDB        GOPERF1
023400,001046:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
023401,001047:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
023402,001048:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23
023403,001049:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF TERM  WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
023404,001050:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
023405,001051:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023406,001052:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023407,001053:                                                                                                  #    N.A.
023408,001054:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED-
023409,001055:                                                                                                  #    ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
023410,001056: 24,3220     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
023411,001057: 24,3220                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
023412,001058: 24,3220           05506        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
023413,001059: 24,3221           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
023414,001060: 24,3222           00004                           INHINT                                         
023415,001061: 24,3223           04665                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
023416,001062: 24,3224           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
023417,001063: 24,3225           00003                           RELINT                                         
023418,001064: 24,3226           34727        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
023419,001065: 24,3227           00006                           EXTEND                                         
023420,001066: 24,3230           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
023421,001067: 24,3231           33270                           CAF      OCT205                                
023422,001068: 24,3232           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
023423,001069: 24,3233           20635                           CADR     GOPERF1                               
023424,001070: 24,3234           03261                           TC       R23LEM2                               #  TERMINATE
023425,001071: 24,3235           03237                           TC       R23LEM11                              #  PROCEDE
023426,001072: 24,3236           03264                           TC       R23LEM3                               #  ENTER- DO ANOTHER MANUVER
023427,001073: 24,3237           00004        R23LEM11           INHINT                                         
023428,001074: 24,3240           04514                           TC       RRLIMCHK                              #  YES - CHECK IF ANTENNA IS WITHIN LIMITS
023429,001075: 24,3241           00035                           ADRES    CDUT                                  
023430,001076: 24,3242           03251                           TC       OUTOFLIM                              #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023431,001077: 24,3243           04665                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  RESTORE DEADBAND TO
023432,001078: 24,3244           40115                           CADR     RESTORDB                              #  ASTRONAUT SELECTED VALUE
023433,001079: 24,3245           00003                           RELINT                                         
023434,001080: 24,3246           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  CLEAR NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
023435,001081: 24,3247           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
023436,001082: 24,3250           02241                           TC       P20LEMB1                              #  RADAR IS LOCKED ON CONTINUE IN P20

023439,001085: 24,3252           33267                           CAF      OCT501PV

023441,001087: 24,3254           21572                           CADR     PRIOLARM                              #  LIMITS

023458,001104:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
023459,001105:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023460,001106:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023461,001107:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
023462,001108:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023463,001109: 
023464,001110:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
023465,001111:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
023466,001112:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
023467,001113:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
023468,001114:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
023469,001115:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
023470,001116:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
023471,001117:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
023472,001118:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023473,001119:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
023474,001120:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
023475,001121:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
023476,001122:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023477,001123:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
023478,001124:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
023479,001125:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
023480,001126:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023481,001127:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023482,001128:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
023483,001129:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
023484,001130:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023485,001131:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
023486,001132:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023487,001133:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
023488,001134: 24,3271  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
023489,001135: 24,3271                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
023490,001136: 24,3271           05506        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
023491,001137: 24,3272           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
023492,001138: 24,3273           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
023493,001139: 24,3274           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
023494,001140: 24,3275           34746        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
023495,001141: 24,3276           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
023496,001142: 24,3277           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
023497,001143: 24,3300           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
023498,001144: 24,3301           05355        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
023499,001145: 24,3302           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
023500,001146: 24,3303           33336                           CAF      V16N80                                
023501,001147: 24,3304           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
023502,001148: 24,3305           20477                           CADR     PRIODSPR                              
023503,001149: 24,3306           06043                           TC       GOTOV56                               
023504,001150: 24,3307           03313                           TC       R24END                                #  PROCEED EXIT R24 TO P20LEM1
023505,001151: 
023506,001152: 24,3310           03317                           TC       R24LEM3                               #  RECYCLE - CALL R61 TO MANEUVER S/C

023562,001208:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
023563,001209:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

023568,001214:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
023569,001215:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
023570,001216:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
023571,001217:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE.

023584,001230:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS FLAG ARE NOT SET.

023773,001419:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023774,001420: 
023775,001421:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023776,001422:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023777,001423:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023778,001424:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023779,001425:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023780,001426:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023781,001427:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023782,001428:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023783,001429:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023784,001430:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023785,001431:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023786,001432:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023787,001433:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023788,001434:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023789,001435:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023790,001436: 
023791,001437:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023792,001438:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023793,001439:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023794,001440: 
023795,001441:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023796,001442:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023797,001443:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023798,001444:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023799,001445: 
023800,001446:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
023801,001447: 
023802,001448:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023803,001449: 
023804,001450:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023805,001451: 
023806,001452:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023807,001453:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023808,001454: 
023809,001455:    4514           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND                                         
023810,001456:    4515           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
023811,001457:    4516           50000                           INDEX    0

023818,001464:    4524           70110                           MASK     RADMODES

023852,001498:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023853,001499: 
023854,001500:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023855,001501:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023856,001502:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023857,001503:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023858,001504:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023859,001505:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023860,001506:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023861,001507:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023862,001508:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023863,001509:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023864,001510:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023865,001511:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023866,001512:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023867,001513:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023868,001514:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023869,001515:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023870,001516:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023871,001517:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023872,001518:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023873,001519:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023874,001520: 
023875,001521:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:

023922,001568:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON

A vertical line is drawn next to the log section name and program name. 

023924,001570: 
023925,001571:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023926,001572: 
023927,001573:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WTIH
023928,001574:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023929,001575:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023930,001576:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023931,001577:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023932,001578:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023933,001579:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023934,001580:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023935,001581:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023936,001582:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023937,001583:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023938,001584:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023939,001585: 
023940,001586:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023941,001587:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
023942,001588:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023943,001589: 
023944,001590:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023945,001591:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023946,001592: 
023947,001593:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023948,001594: 
023949,001595:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023950,001596:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023951,001597: 
023952,001598:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023953,001599: 
023954,001600:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023955,001601: 
023956,001602: 24,3337                                           BANK     24                                    
023957,001603: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023958,001604: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023959,001605: 
023960,001606: 25,2053  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023961,001607: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023962,001608: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB

023964,001610: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.

023971,001617:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023972,001618: 
023973,001619:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023974,001620:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023975,001621:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023976,001622:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023977,001623:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023978,001624:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
023979,001625:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023980,001626:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023981,001627:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023982,001628:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023983,001629:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023984,001630:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023985,001631:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023986,001632:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023987,001633:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023988,001634:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023989,001635: 
023990,001636:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023991,001637:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023992,001638:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023993,001639: 
023994,001640:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023995,001641: 
023996,001642:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023997,001643:                                                                                                  #  NONE

024044,001690:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
024045,001691:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024046,001692:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024047,001693:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
024048,001694:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
024049,001695:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
024050,001696:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
024051,001697:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
024052,001698:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
024053,001699:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
024054,001700:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
024055,001701:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
024056,001702:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
024057,001703:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
024058,001704:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
024059,001705:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
024060,001706:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
024061,001707:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
024062,001708:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
024063,001709:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024064,001710:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
024065,001711:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
024066,001712:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
024067,001713:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
024068,001714: 
024069,001715:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024070,001716:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
024071,001717:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
024072,001718: 
024073,001719:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024074,001720:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024075,001721: 
024076,001722:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024077,001723:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
024078,001724: 
024079,001725:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024080,001726:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024081,001727: 
024082,001728:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
024083,001729:

024131,001777:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
024132,001778: 
024133,001779:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
024134,001780:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
024135,001781:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
024136,001782:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
024137,001783:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
024138,001784:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
024139,001785:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
024140,001786:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024141,001787:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
024142,001788:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
024143,001789:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
024144,001790:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024145,001791:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
024146,001792:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
024147,001793:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
024148,001794:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
024149,001795:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
024150,001796:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
024151,001797:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
024152,001798:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
024153,001799: 
024154,001800:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024155,001801:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
024156,001802:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
024157,001803:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
024158,001804:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
024159,001805: 
024160,001806:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024161,001807:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024162,001808: 
024163,001809:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024164,001810:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
024165,001811:

024167,001813:                                                                                                  #  NONE

024223,001869:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
024224,001870: 
024225,001871:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024226,001872:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
024227,001873:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
024228,001874:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
024229,001875:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
024230,001876:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
024231,001877:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
024232,001878:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
024233,001879:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
024234,001880:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
024235,001881:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
024236,001882:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
024237,001883:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
024238,001884:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
024239,001885:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
024240,001886: 
024241,001887:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
024242,001888:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
024243,001889:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
024244,001890:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
024245,001891:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
024246,001892: 
024247,001893:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024248,001894:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
024249,001895: 
024250,001896:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_

024255,001901:

024257,001903:

024259,001905:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)

024311,001957:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
024312,001958: 
024313,001959:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024314,001960:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
024315,001961:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
024316,001962:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
024317,001963:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
024318,001964:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
024319,001965:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
024320,001966:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
024321,001967:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
024322,001968:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
024323,001969:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
024324,001970:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
024325,001971:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
024326,001972:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024327,001973: 
024328,001974:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024329,001975:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
024330,001976:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
024331,001977: 
024332,001978:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024333,001979:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
024334,001980:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
024335,001981:
