024417,002063:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
024418,002064: 
024419,002065:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024420,002066:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
024421,002067:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
024422,002068:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
024423,002069:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
024424,002070:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
024425,002071:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
024426,002072:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
024427,002073:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
024428,002074:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
024429,002075:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
024430,002076:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
024431,002077:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
024432,002078:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
024433,002079:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
024434,002080:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
024435,002081:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
024436,002082:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
024437,002083:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
024438,002084:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
024439,002085:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
024440,002086:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
024441,002087:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
024442,002088: 
024443,002089:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024444,002090:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
024445,002091:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
024446,002092:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024447,002093:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024448,002094: 
024449,002095:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024450,002096:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
024451,002097: 
024452,002098:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024453,002099:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
024454,002100:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
024455,002101: 
024456,002102:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024457,002103:                                                                                                  #     NONE
024458,002104: 
024459,002105:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024460,002106: 
024461,002107:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
024462,002108:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
024463,002109:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.

024503,002149:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
024504,002150: 
024505,002151:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
024506,002152:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
024507,002153:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024508,002154:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
024509,002155:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
024510,002156:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024511,002157:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
024512,002158:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
024513,002159:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
024514,002160:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
024515,002161:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
024516,002162:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
024517,002163:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
024518,002164:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
024519,002165:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
024520,002166:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
024521,002167:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
024522,002168:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
024523,002169:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
024524,002170:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
024525,002171:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024526,002172: 
024527,002173:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024528,002174:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
024529,002175: 
024530,002176:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024531,002177:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
024532,002178: 
024533,002179:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024534,002180:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR, WAITLIST
024535,002181: 
024536,002182:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024537,002183:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES
024538,002184:

024540,002186:

024675,002321:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024676,002322: 
024677,002323:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024678,002324:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024679,002325:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024680,002326:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024681,002327:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024682,002328:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024683,002329:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024684,002330:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024685,002331:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024686,002332:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024687,002333:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024688,002334:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024689,002335:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024690,002336:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024691,002337:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024692,002338:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024693,002339:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024694,002340:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024695,002341:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024696,002342:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024697,002343:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024698,002344:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024699,002345:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024700,002346:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024701,002347:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024702,002348:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024703,002349: 
024704,002350:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024705,002351:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024706,002352:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024707,002353:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024708,002354: 
024709,002355:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024710,002356:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024711,002357: 
024712,002358:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024713,002359:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024714,002360: 
024715,002361:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024716,002362: 
024717,002363:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024718,002364:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024719,002365: 
024720,002366:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024721,002367:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024722,002368:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024723,002369: 
024724,002370: 25,2564           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

024770,002416:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024771,002417: 
024772,002418:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024773,002419:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024774,002420:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024775,002421:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024776,002422:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024777,002423:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024778,002424:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024779,002425:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024780,002426:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024781,002427:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
024782,002428:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024783,002429:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024784,002430:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
024785,002431:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024786,002432:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024787,002433:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024788,002434:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024789,002435:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024790,002436:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024791,002437:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024792,002438:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024793,002439:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024794,002440:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024795,002441:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024796,002442:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024797,002443:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024798,002444:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024799,002445:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024800,002446:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024801,002447:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024802,002448:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024803,002449:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024804,002450:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024805,002451:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024806,002452:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024807,002453:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024808,002454:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024809,002455:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024810,002456: 
024811,002457:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024812,002458:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024813,002459: 
024814,002460:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024815,002461:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024816,002462:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024817,002463: 
024818,002464:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024819,002465:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

025102,002748:                                                                                                  #  RADAR RUPT READER (R20)
025103,002749: 
025104,002750:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE, WHICH IS INITIATED BY A RADAR RUPT, PROCESSES THE RADAR DATA AND UPDATES THE APPROPRIATE
025105,002751:                                                                                                  #  DSKY LIGHTS.
025106,002752: 
025107,002753: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   RADARUPT

025111,002757: 
025112,002758: 25,3157  E7,1453                                  EBANK=   TTOGO                                 
025113,002759: 
025114,002760: 25,3157           00006        RADAREAD           EXTEND                                         #  CONTINUATION OF INTERRUPT LEAD-IN.
025115,002761: 25,3160           04007                           ROR      SUPERBNK                              #  SUPERBNK MUST BE SAVED BECAUSE RUPT
025116,002762: 25,3161           54016                           TS       BANKRUPT                              #  MAY EXIT VIA TASKOVER.
025117,002763: 25,3162           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025118,002764: 25,3163           22012                           QXCH     QRUPT                                 
025119,002765: 
025120,002766: 
025121,002767: 25,3164           34750                           CA       SEVEN                                 #  READ AND STORE RADAR SELECT BITS
025122,002768: 25,3165           00006                           EXTEND

025125,002771: 
025126,002772: 25,3170           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  IF RADAR SELECT BITS ARE ZERO, ALARM
025127,002773: 25,3171           13177                           BZF      BADRUPT                               #  WITHOUT READING DATA
025128,002774: 
025129,002775: 25,3172           30046                           CA       RNRAD                                 #  STORE RAW DATA FOR DOWNLINK.
025130,002776: 25,3173           51332                           INDEX    RADBITS

025132,002778:

025596,003242:

025747,003393:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025748,003394:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025749,003395: 
025750,003396: 
025751,003397:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025752,003398: 
025753,003399:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025754,003400:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025755,003401:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025756,003402: 
025757,003403:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025758,003404: 
025759,003405: 
025760,003406:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025761,003407: 
025762,003408: 
025763,003409:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025764,003410: 
025765,003411:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT    LPS20.1
025766,003412:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025767,003413:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025768,003414:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025769,003415:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025770,003416: 
025771,003417: 
025772,003418:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025773,003419: 
025774,003420:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025775,003421:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025776,003422: 
025777,003423: 
025778,003424:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025779,003425:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025780,003426: 
025781,003427: 
025782,003428:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025783,003429:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025784,003430: 
025785,003431:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025786,003432: 
025787,003433:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025788,003434:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025789,003435:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025790,003436:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
025791,003437:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
025792,003438: 
025793,003439: 
025794,003440:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025795,003441: 
025796,003442:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 588 

025798,003444:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
025799,003445:                                                                                                  #      2)RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
025800,003446: 
025801,003447:                                                                                                  #     THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX,CDUY,CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
025802,003448: 
025803,003449:

026015,003661:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
026016,003662:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
026017,003663:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
026018,003664: 
026019,003665:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026020,003666: 
026021,003667:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
026022,003668:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
026023,003669:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
026024,003670: 
026025,003671:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
026026,003672:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
026027,003673:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
026028,003674:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
026029,003675:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
026030,003676:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
026031,003677:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
026032,003678: 
026033,003679: 
026034,003680:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026035,003681:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
026036,003682:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
026037,003683: 
026038,003684:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026039,003685:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026040,003686:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026041,003687:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026042,003688:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026043,003689:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026044,003690: 
026045,003691: 
026046,003692:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026047,003693:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026048,003694:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026049,003695:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026050,003696:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026051,003697:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
026052,003698:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
026053,003699:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
026054,003700:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
026055,003701:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
026056,003702:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
026057,003703:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
026058,003704:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
026059,003705:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
026060,003706:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026061,003707: 
026062,003708:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026063,003709:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
026064,003710:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

Page 595 

026066,003712:                                                                                                  #   ULC,RXZ,SINTHETA,LGRET,RDRET,BVECTOR,W.IND,X78T

026455,004101: 26,3205           50644                                    R22LEM93                              
026456,004102:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026457,004103: 
026458,004104:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
026459,004105:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
026460,004106:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
026461,004107: 
026462,004108:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026463,004109:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
026464,004110:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
026465,004111: 
026466,004112:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026467,004113:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026468,004114:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026469,004115:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026470,004116:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026471,004117:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026472,004118:

Page 603 

026474,004120:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026475,004121:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026476,004122:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026477,004123:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026478,004124:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026479,004125:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
026480,004126:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026481,004127:

026687,004333:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
026688,004334:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
026689,004335: 
026690,004336: 
026691,004337:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026692,004338: 
026693,004339:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026694,004340:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026695,004341:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026696,004342:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026697,004343: 
026698,004344: 
026699,004345:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026700,004346: 
026701,004347: 
026702,004348:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026703,004349: 
026704,004350:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026705,004351:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026706,004352:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026707,004353:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026708,004354:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026709,004355: 
026710,004356: 
026711,004357:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -  TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026712,004358: 
026713,004359: 
026714,004360:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026715,004361: 
026716,004362:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026717,004363:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026718,004364:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026719,004365: 
026720,004366:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026721,004367:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026722,004368:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026723,004369:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026724,004370: 
026725,004371:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026726,004372:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026727,004373:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026728,004374:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026729,004375:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026730,004376: 
026731,004377: 
026732,004378: 26,3441                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
026733,004379: 26,3441           34746        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO
